ENTRY       EC 2.1.1.185                Enzyme
NAME        23S rRNA (guanosine2251-2'-O)-methyltransferase;
            rlmB (gene name);
            yifH (gene name)
CLASS       Transferases;
            Transferring one-carbon groups;
            Methyltransferases
SYSNAME     S-adenosyl-L-methionine:23S rRNA (guanosine2251-2'-O-)-methyltransferase
REACTION    S-adenosyl-L-methionine + guanosine2251 in 23S rRNA = S-adenosyl-L-homocysteine + 2'-O-methylguanosine2251 in 23S rRNA
SUBSTRATE   S-adenosyl-L-methionine [CPD:C00019];
            guanosine2251 in 23S rRNA
PRODUCT     S-adenosyl-L-homocysteine [CPD:C00021];
            2'-O-methylguanosine2251 in 23S rRNA
COMMENT     The enzyme catalyses the methylation of guanosine2251, a modification conserved in the peptidyltransferase domain of 23S rRNA.
HISTORY     EC 2.1.1.185 created 2010
REFERENCE   1  [PMID:11698387]
  AUTHORS   Lovgren JM, Wikstrom PM

  JOURNAL   J Bacteriol 183:6957-60 (2001)
            DOI:10.1128/JB.183.23.6957-6960.2001
  SEQUENCE  [eco:b4180]
